Calculation Trail (every step, every number)
Step 1 — Pi Ratings
formula: composite = (home_rating + away_rating) / 2
Argentina: home_rating=0.9365, away_rating=-0.0937 → composite = (0.9365 + -0.0937) / 2 = 0.4214 (from 12 matches)
Austria: home_rating=0.3000, away_rating=-0.0300 → composite = (0.3000 + -0.0300) / 2 = 0.1350 (from 1 matches)
Step 2 — Calibration Parameters
total_anchor = 3.0250 (fitted, n=40 2026 matches)
rho = -0.1600 (fitted) — Dixon-Coles low-score correlation
Step 3 — Lambdas (Expected Goals per Team)
formula: margin = home_composite − away_composite
formula: λ_H = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 + margin/2)
formula: λ_A = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 − margin/2)
margin = 0.4214 − 0.1350 = 0.2864
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.0250/2 + 0.2864/2) = 1.6557
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.0250/2 − 0.2864/2) = 1.3693
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
With λ_H=1.6557, λ_A=1.3693, ρ=-0.1600:
τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.6557×1.3693×(-0.1600) = 1.3627
Grid sum = 1.000000 (should be ≈1.000000)
E[home goals] = 1.6557, E[away goals] = 1.3693
Step 5 — Market Derivations (cell summation)
home_win = Σ P(h,a) for h > a = 0.4253
draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2744
away_win = Σ P(h,a) for h < a = 0.3002
over_2.5 = Σ P(h,a) for h+a > 2.5 = 0.5824
btts_yes = Σ P(h,a) for h≥1 AND a≥1 = 0.6209

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

margin = -0.0331 − -0.1132 = 0.0801
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.0250/2 + 0.0801/2) = 1.5526
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.0250/2 − 0.0801/2) = 1.4724
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
With λ_H=1.5526, λ_A=1.4724, ρ=-0.1600:
τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.5526×1.4724×(-0.1600) = 1.3658
Grid sum = 1.000000 (should be ≈1.000000)
E[home goals] = 1.5526, E[away goals] = 1.4724

home_win = Σ P(h,a) for h > a = 0.3790
draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2772

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
